 Walking on the red carpet is associated with fame, special events, honors, etc
 lekin raajnneeti main kabhi-kabhi aapke liye dikkat kaa kaaran bhi ban saktaa he, jaisaa haal hi main punjab ke mukhyamantri captain amarinder singh ke saath hua
 Actually, after the grenade attack on Nirankari Bhavan in Amritsar, the red carpet was laid for Amarinder Singh at the scene
 haalanki vivaad badhane ke baad ise hataaya gaya
 The red carpet is laid on special occasions, but have you ever wondered when this red carpet started? Although this royal tradition started from outside, but India tops in making handmade carpets
 kaha jaataa he ki bharat handmad carpet banane main pehle sthaan par he or utpaadan kaa 70-80 fisadi hissaa niryaat kar diya jaataa he
 It is easily available in India and is used in many ceremonies
 amritsar hamalaa: amarinder ke liye bicha red carpet, daure se pehle hatayakaha jaataa he ki yah aam janata ke liye nahin, balki khaas logon ke liye iskaa istemaal kiya jaataa rahaa he
 If we talk about history, the earliest mention of this is found in the Greek drama Agamemnon of Esquilus
 yah us vakt kii baat he jab gautam buddha the or magadh ke ajatshatru bharat ke sabase shaktishaalee raja the
 The play shows the Greek king Agamemnon leave his wife at home to go to war
 yah yuddh lambey samay tak chalata he or donon raja or rani ek- duusare ke liye vafaadaar nahin rahete hai
 Later, when he returns to his country after winning the war, he returns with a woman
 haalanki, phir bhi rani clitenestra apane vijayi pati ke liye laal kaaleen bichaati hai
 However, he does not want to walk on that carpet, because according to Greek beliefs, only God can walk on the red carpet
 lekin rani ke kehane par wo red carpet par chalate hai
 Since then the red carpet has moved from Greece to other countries
 vahiin aadhikarik taur par sabase pehali baar red carpet kaa istemaal saal 1821 main hua tha, jab tatkaaleen raashtrapati james moroy ke swaagat main yah bichaaya gaya tha
 Then in the year 1902 the red carpet was used for the passengers of the New Express train in New York
 uske baad 1920 ke baad se yah hollywood or fishan event main aam ho gaya
 When did the red carpet come to India? If we talk about India, there is no specific mention of when it was used for the first time in India
 haalanki kaha jaataa he ki iskaa istemaal saal 1911 main dilli darbar main hua tha, jab tatkaaleen waisaroy lord hardinge ne king jorge ve ke liye yah bichhawaya tha
 It was located in the Darbarlal fort and special arrangements were made for it at that time and the forest inside the Red Fort was cleaned and used for Queen Mary with King George V
 haalanki ab koi videshi mahamaan ke liye raashtrapati bhawan, loksabhaa or rajyasabha main bhi iskaa istemaal kiya jaataa he
